## <a name="windows-server-2012-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeae5-1515">Atributos do Windows Server 2012</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeae5-1515">Windows Server 2012 Attributes</span></span>
